# IVS, Base Character & Variation Selector Usage Statistics
#
# The first row reports the total number of unique IVSes; the second row
# reports the total number of unique base characters; the rows that begin
# with 'VS' followed by an integer report the total number of unique IVSes
# using a particular variation selector; and subsequent rows that simply
# begin with an integer value report the number of base characters which
# include that particular number of IVSes.
#
# 1st Column: Identifies the type of information; value can be 'IVS',
#             'BC' (base character), a short name for a VS in the form
#             'VSnn' or 'VSnnn', or an integer value
# 2nd Column: Sum total for each column statistics
# 3rd Column: Data for the Adobe-Japan1 collection
# 4th Column: Data for the Hanyo-Denshi collection
# 5th Column: Data for the Moji_Joho collection
# 6th Column: Data for the PanCJKV collection
#
# Additional columns will be defined as new collections are added.
#
# Duplicate sequence identifiers and shared IVSes are reported in comments
# at the end of the file.
#
# This file is part of the Unicode Ideographic Variation Database (IVD).
# For more details on the IVD, see UTS #37:
# http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr37/
#

# For terms of use, see: http://www.unicode.org/terms_of_use.html
